Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

  if (!PortTopologyMatches(isolate, context, inputs, inputs_)) {                  // *** 5 ***

<br>





The root cause of this vulnerability is JavaScript callback from [1].



<span class="line"><!---->The root cause of this vulnerability is JavaScript callback from [1].<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In `AudioWorkletProcessor::PortTopologyMatches`, `audio_port_1` is the parameter variable `inputs` in `AudioWorkletProcessor::Process` [5].



<span class="line"><!---->In `AudioWorkletProcessor::PortTopologyMatches`, `audio_port_1` is the parameter variable `inputs` in `AudioWorkletProcessor::Process` [5].<!----></span>



<br>





The size of `audio_port_1` is the same as the length of `audio_bus_2` in most cases.



<span class="line"><!---->The size of `audio_port_1` is the same as the length of `audio_bus_2` in most cases.<!----></span>



<br>





The variable `audio_bus_2` is determined by `audio_port_1` in `AudioWorkletProcessor::ClonePortTopology` function.



<span class="line"><!---->The variable `audio_bus_2` is determined by `audio_port_1` in `AudioWorkletProcessor::ClonePortTopology` function.<!----></span>



<br>





After `audio_bus_2` is set, `audio_bus_2` is not changed before `AudioWorkletProcessor::PortTopologyMatches` returns `false`.



<span class="line"><!---->After `audio_bus_2` is set, `audio_bus_2` is not changed before `AudioWorkletProcessor::PortTopologyMatches` returns `false`.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





When the user makes two `AudioWorkletNode`s using singleton pattern, `AudioWorkletNode`s have the same `AudioWorkletProcessor`.



<span class="line"><!---->When the user makes two `AudioWorkletNode`s using singleton pattern, `AudioWorkletNode`s have the same `AudioWorkletProcessor`.<!----></span>



<br>





Then, `AudioWorkletProcessor::PortTopologyMatches` can have different sizes of `audio_port_1`.



<span class="line"><!---->Then, `AudioWorkletProcessor::PortTopologyMatches` can have different sizes of `audio_port_1`.<!----></span>



<br>





Because we can pass the different sizes of `inputs` using different `AudioWorkletNode`s.



<span class="line"><!---->Because we can pass the different sizes of `inputs` using different `AudioWorkletNode`s.<!----></span>



<br>





It means that the length of `port_2_local` less than `bus_index_counter` which is an index of `audio_port_1`'s size.



<span class="line"><!---->It means that the length of `port_2_local` less than `bus_index_counter` which is an index of `audio_port_1`'s size.<!----></span>



<br>





In this case, we can make a JavaScript callback using `__defineGetter__`, and it will be called in [1].



<span class="line"><!---->In this case, we can make a JavaScript callback using `__defineGetter__`, and it will be called in [1].<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Using the JavaScript callback, we can control the variable `value` which is the return value of the callback. 



<span class="line"><!---->Using the JavaScript callback, we can control the variable `value` which is the return value of the callback. <!----></span>



<br>





Then, we can bypass the check routine [2] because we can control the size of the array using the callback.



<span class="line"><!---->Then, we can bypass the check routine [2] because we can control the size of the array using the callback.<!----></span>



<br>





Also, we can bypass the check routines [3], and [4] in the same manner.



<span class="line"><!---->Also, we can bypass the check routines [3], and [4] in the same manner.<!----></span>



<br>





Bypassing the check routines, `AudioWorkletProcessor::PortTopologyMatches` always returns `true`.



<span class="line"><!---->Bypassing the check routines, `AudioWorkletProcessor::PortTopologyMatches` always returns `true`.<!----></span>



<br>





It means the variable `audio_bus_2` is never changed, and also the variable `array_buffers`, which is explained as follows, is not changed too.



<span class="line"><!---->It means the variable `audio_bus_2` is never changed, and also the variable `array_buffers`, which is explained as follows, is not changed too.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In `AudioWorkletProcessor::CopyPortToArrayBuffers`, `audio_port` is the same variable above `audio_port_1`.



<span class="line"><!---->In `AudioWorkletProcessor::CopyPortToArrayBuffers`, `audio_port` is the same variable above `audio_port_1`.<!----></span>



<br>





The variable `array_buffers` is `Vector` type, and the size of `array_buffers` is also determined by `audio_port_1` from `AudioWorkletProcessor::ClonePortTopology`.



<span class="line"><!---->The variable `array_buffers` is `Vector` type, and the size of `array_buffers` is also determined by `audio_port_1` from `AudioWorkletProcessor::ClonePortTopology`.<!----></span>



<br>





It means that the size of `audio_port_1` can be bigger than the size of `array_buffers` (using singleton pattern and bypassing check routines). 



<span class="line"><!---->It means that the size of `audio_port_1` can be bigger than the size of `array_buffers` (using singleton pattern and bypassing check routines). <!----></span>



<br>





So we can access `array_buffers` out of bounds in [6].



<span class="line"><!---->So we can access `array_buffers` out of bounds in [6].<!----></span>



<br>





Also, if we detach one of `ArrayBuffer` in `array_buffers` from `AudioWorkletProcessor::PortTopologyMatches` after bypassing check routines (TOCTOU), 



<span class="line"><!---->Also, if we detach one of `ArrayBuffer` in `array_buffers` from `AudioWorkletProcessor::PortTopologyMatches` after bypassing check routines (TOCTOU), <!----></span>



<br>





We can access the detached backing store of `ArrayBuffer` in [7]. 



<span class="line"><!---->We can access the detached backing store of `ArrayBuffer` in [7]. <!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>



<br>

<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





Chrome Version: 90.0.4430.72  (latest stable version)



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome Version: 90.0.4430.72  (latest stable version)<!----></span>



<br>





Operating System: Windows, Linux, MacOS, Android



<span class="line"><!---->Operating System: Windows, Linux, MacOS, Android<!----></span>

REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>



<br>





I attached two JavaScript codes. One is Out-of-Bounds `Vector` access. The other is accessing the detached `ArrayBuffer`'s backing store.



<span class="line"><!---->I attached two JavaScript codes. One is Out-of-Bounds `Vector` access. The other is accessing the detached `ArrayBuffer`'s backing store.<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->Please see the attachments.<!----></span>

Return false when the size of audio_port_1 and audio_port_2 is different



<span class="line"><!---->Return false when the size of audio_port_1 and audio_port_2 is different<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The current code assumes the size of audio ports is identical because



<span class="line"><!---->The current code assumes the size of audio ports is identical because<!----></span>



<br>





the number of inputs and outputs cannot change after construction. This



<span class="line"><!---->the number of inputs and outputs cannot change after construction. This<!----></span>



<br>





assumption is broken when multiple AudioWorkletNodes share a singleton



<span class="line"><!---->assumption is broken when multiple AudioWorkletNodes share a singleton<!----></span>



<br>





AudioWorkletProcessor instance.



<span class="line"><!---->AudioWorkletProcessor instance.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This patch removes the assumption and explicitly returns false when the



<span class="line"><!---->This patch removes the assumption and explicitly returns false when the<!----></span>



<br>





number of inputs and outputs does not match.



<span class="line"><!---->number of inputs and outputs does not match.<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

[M90-LTS] Return false when the size of audio_port_1 and audio_port_2 is different



<span class="line"><!---->[M90-LTS] Return false when the size of audio_port_1 and audio_port_2 is different<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The current code assumes the size of audio ports is identical because



<span class="line"><!---->The current code assumes the size of audio ports is identical because<!----></span>



<br>





the number of inputs and outputs cannot change after construction. This



<span class="line"><!---->the number of inputs and outputs cannot change after construction. This<!----></span>



<br>





assumption is broken when multiple AudioWorkletNodes share a singleton



<span class="line"><!---->assumption is broken when multiple AudioWorkletNodes share a singleton<!----></span>



<br>





AudioWorkletProcessor instance.



<span class="line"><!---->AudioWorkletProcessor instance.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This patch removes the assumption and explicitly returns false when the



<span class="line"><!---->This patch removes the assumption and explicitly returns false when the<!----></span>



<br>





number of inputs and outputs does not match.



<span class="line"><!---->number of inputs and outputs does not match.<!----></span>
